	var drawing=document.getElementById("myCanvas");
	if (drawing.getContext){
		var ctx = drawing.getContext("2d");
        var index = 0;
        function heart(){
		var arrays = data["shapes"];
		var pos = arrays[index]["data"];
		var color = arrays[index]["color"];
		var type = arrays[index]["type"];
		switch(type){
		case 1: 
		ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(" + color[0] + ", "+ color[1] + ",  "+ color[2] + ", " + color[3] / 255 + ")";
		
		ctx.fillRect (pos[0] * 2, pos[1] * 2,(pos[2] - pos[0]) * 2, (pos[3] - pos[1]) * 2);
		break;
		case 32:
          ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(" + color[0] + ", "+ color[1] + ",  "+ color[2] + ", " + color[3] / 255 + ")";
		   ctx.beginPath();
		   ctx.arc(pos[0] * 2,pos[1] * 2,pos[2] * 2,0,2*Math.PI);
		   ctx.fill();
		   break;
		   }
         
            index++;
            if (index > arrays.length){ // 
                clearInterval(intervalId);
            }
        }
        intervalId = setInterval(heart,300);  //100ms
	}
	
	</script>
